# Batch 11 Status Ledger - Image Coverage And Release QA

Purpose: track image-level reconstruction proof for every approved `Covered` / `Covered/Adjusted` target in `image-coverage-map.md`.

Readiness audit: `batch-11-readiness-audit.md`.

Status definitions:

- `Aprovado`: image coverage story uses only approved library components, matches the approved full image visually, has screenshot/measurement evidence, has no overflow, and passed required validation.
- `Semi-aprovada`: image coverage story exists, renders with official reusable components, has no smoke/overflow blocker, and is acceptable for product review, but is not certified 1:1.
- `Em ajuste`: image coverage story exists and renders, but visual review or comparison still has unresolved mismatch.
- `Implementado sem certificacao`: story exists but has not completed full-image screenshot comparison/review.
- `Nao iniciado`: no image coverage story exists yet.
- `Ignorada`: product decision says this image should not consume implementation/certification work.

Batch 11 rule:

- No image row can be marked `Aprovado` while its composition depends on one-off screen markup for a component that should live in the library.
- Image coverage stories are proof compositions only. They may position approved components, but must not replace component internals with screen-specific markup.

## Internal Consumer Readiness

Current status: in progress. The goal is to make the already-certified internal components usable by `C:\Users\lucas\taliya-internal` without importing story/demo markup or recreating local CSS. Product decision on 2026-06-18: do not create or promote a separate `InternalShell`; use the same configurable `CrmProductShell` for CRM and internal/backoffice, with `InternalOverviewDashboard` as page content.

Source diagnostic before code edits:

- Source image: `48_round-4.1K_internal_01_visao-operacional.png.png`.
- Certified component crop: `tmp/visual-audit/batch10/support-internal-sources/image48-internal-shell-broad.png`.
- Certified render evidence: historical capture `tmp/visual-audit/batch10/support-internal-final-20260531/InternalShell.png`; the certified content is now named `InternalOverviewDashboard`.
- Visual anatomy: header/actions, filter row, six operational cards, activity panel, and copiloto panel already match the Batch 10 content crop and must remain stable.
- Consumer mismatch: the old internal dashboard/shell boundary hardcoded title, subtitle, action buttons, search/filter row, dashboard cards, activity rows, copiloto copy and action labels. `taliya-internal` needs to pass prepared operational data/callbacks from its `OperationalView` and route state into `CrmProductShell` and `InternalOverviewDashboard` rather than copy CSS or rebuild the component locally.
- Owner: `@taliya/crm` public component API and stories/tests. No token or primitive visual change is expected for the first probe.
- Smallest probe: add region flags and slots to `CrmProductShell`, keep the default CRM render visually unchanged, expose prepared internal content through `InternalOverviewDashboard`, and add a configured consumer story plus focused tests. If the default source story shifts visually, revert the structural part and split the API work into narrower props.

2026-06-12 update: official Hoje shell behavior changed to browser-level vertical scroll, not `.tcrm-product-shell-content` scroll. Sidebar must not scroll; it is compacted by official sidebar spacing tokens and must fit within `100vh`. `ActivityFeed` remains an official CRM component, not a page-only implementation, and now uses product shell surface/control/row tokens plus image-20-derived density tokens. The `?image=20` preview no longer auto-scrolls; use the browser scrollbar to reach the continuation naturally.

2026-06-15 filter architecture update: global dropdown filters must use official filter primitives, not form `Select`, cycling buttons, or page-local popovers. `FilterSelect` is single-value and uses Radix Select semantics; `FilterMultiSelect` is multi-value and uses a listbox popover with clear/apply behavior. Both must cover empty, selected, open, hover, focus, loading, disabled, empty-options, real popup, and official product-shell surface/border/shadow/typography tokens. Image 21 operation filters use `FilterSelect` for simple filters and `FilterMultiSelect` for multi filters; image 20 `ActivityFeed` history filters use `FilterSelect`; `Select` remains reserved for form fields.

2026-06-15 filter quality correction: `FilterSelect` and `FilterMultiSelect` must follow mature dropdown/listbox anatomy: pill trigger, compact header, scrollable option list, row hover, row selected state, fixed check mark slot, optional description/count badge, clear action, and footer apply action for multi-select. The selected option mark must never render as a full-width bar or high-contrast block; selected emphasis belongs to the row background and check glyph. The trigger must render the label/value separator as real markup, not as a spacing-sensitive pseudo-element. All filter text must consume `--taliya-type-font-primary`; current repo does not include a licensed Lufga font asset, so Storybook will fall back to the next family until the real font file is added or the primary family is officially changed.

2026-06-15 filter contract correction: the previous compact-header/footer/count-badge dropdown direction was rejected in review. The accepted global filter primitive contract is now: trigger pill with label, selected chips/value, clear `x` inside the trigger when selected, and chevron always visible; popup with solid official surface, no title/header, no apply footer, no option descriptions/counts; each option is one full-width menu row with contextual leading icon + name + trailing check icon when selected. Hover/focus/selected backgrounds must apply to the row only. This applies globally to `FilterSelect` and `FilterMultiSelect`, including Opera��o filters and Hoje history filters.

2026-06-27 Image 20 ActivityFeed token-source correction:

- Source/current diagnostic: opened `20_round-4.1A_hoje_04_historico-de-hoje.png.png` at the approved `1672x941` source viewport and captured the current static render in `tmp/visual-audit/batch11/today-20-current-diagnostic-source-viewport-v1`. Regional diagnostic before code edits:

- Shell/topbar/sidebar: source uses the CRM shell family with active Financeiro sidebar and finance-specific top nav (`Visao geral`, `Kanban`, `Pagamentos`, `Casos`, `Documentos`). Owner: `@taliya/crm` `CrmProductShell` plus story nav/sidebar props.
- Page title/header: source title is `Financeiro`, subtitle is `Filas financeiras e pendencias do estudio`, and actions `Nova cobranca`, `Exportar`, `Criar tarefa` sit in the page header rather than inside the filterbar. Owner: `CrmProductShell` `title`, `subtitle`, `pageHeaderActions`, and official `Button`.
- Filter bar: source has period chips `Hoje`, `Esta semana`, `Este mes` plus selects `Unidade`, `Status`, `Responsavel`, with no search field. Owner: official `PageFilterBar searchVisible=false`, `FilterChip`, and `FilterSelect`.
- Priority strip: source has a titled panel `Prioridades financeiras` with three actionable rows, icon tile, title, amount, metadata and chevron. Owner: official `@taliya/crm` `FinancePriorityPanel`, composed from `Panel`, `PanelHeader`, `Icon`, `EmptyState`, and native source-derived row buttons documented in the primitive-reuse audit.
- Queue grid: source has eight finance queue cards. Owner: certified `PaymentCaseCard` states `due`, `today`, `paid`, `overdue`, `failed`, `reconciliation`, `promise`, and `exception`.
- Accepted probe: removed the image-coverage story's initial selected priority row, moved selected priority into the isolated component variant, reset the finance panel header negative margin/border inherited from `PanelHeader`, and reduced priority-row amount typography from numeric display to body-strong scale. Evidence: `finance-30-priority-panel-v4` and `finance-30-priority-panel-v4-source-size`.
- Accepted probe: tokenized `FinancePriorityPanel` density at 16px padding, 12px gap, and 50px row height, reduced Image 30 page/queue composition gap to 10px, and intentionally left certified `PaymentCaseCard` dimensions unchanged. Evidence: `finance-30-rhythm-v5-source-size` shows `verticalOverflow=0`, `priorityPanel.height=218`, `queues.bottom=903`, and `firstRowCardCount=4`.
- Accepted probe: switched Image 30 header action buttons from `size="sm"` to official default `md` and promoted a reusable stacked-header actions offset token (`26px`) into `CrmProductShell`. Evidence: `finance-30-header-actions-v7` shows actions at `y=155`, buttons at `42px`, unchanged filter/panel/cards, and no overflow.
- Accepted probe: promoted product-shell top-nav rhythm into official tokens after testing `nav458_item42_gap16_pad22` against rejected smaller/wider options. Evidence: `finance-30-topnav-official-v8` shows nav `x=530`, active pill `109x42`, shell item height `42px`, gap `16px`, padding-x `22px`, and unchanged filter/panel/cards with no overflow.
- Accepted probe: removed the incorrect shell-nav capsule surface by making only the shell `SegmentedControl` container background/border transparent and shadowless while preserving the approved 4px container padding. Rejected `transparent-no-padding` because it moved the active pill from `x=535` to `x=531` and shrank the wrapper to `44px` high. Evidence: `finance-30-shell-surface-probes-v1` and official static evidence `finance-30-shell-surface-official-v9`.

## 2026-06-11 Image 76 Diagnostic Update

- Current source/render anatomy check confirms the 76 composition uses the official components: `AccessShell layout=centered`, `SubscriptionResolutionPanel`, `SubscriptionStatusCard state=failed`, `StatusSummaryCard`, `InlineAlert`, `Chip`, `SecurePaymentNotice`, and `Button`.
- Structural status remains stable: card bbox `706x653`, rendered rect `x=483 y=186 width=706 height=653`, and overflow `0x0`.
- Correction to the row above: the active secure content token is `secure-content = rgba(46, 57, 83, 0.48)`; the older `0.52` mention is stale history and must not be reused.
- Accepted new probe: `actionShadowVerySoft`, promoted to failed-state tokens `failed-action-shadow = rgba(16, 20, 26, 0.045)`, `failed-primary-shadow-y = 5px`, and `failed-primary-shadow-blur = 8px`.
- Latest static Storybook recapture after promotion: `mean_abs_channel_diff = 8.0655`, `changed_gt_8 = 0.1135`, `changed_gt_16 = 0.0779`. Region means: header `11.3126`, callout `10.3273`, status row `6.6151`, details `5.3785`, secure `10.6852`, action `13.5211`, footer note `5.8503`.
- Rejected in this diagnostic pass: `secureSourceNeutralA`, `secureSourceNeutralB`, `secureSurfaceWhiter`, `secureNeutralSurface`, `lighterAction`, `softAction`, `actionSourceSoft`, `actionSlightlyLighter`, `actionWeight500`, `actionWeight400`, `actionTranslateDown1`, `actionText15`, `actionText15Weight500`, `actionText15Weight400`, `footerNoteDarker`, `footerNoteBlue`, `failedTitleOffsetMinus10`, `failedTitleOffsetMinus9`, and `failedTitleOffsetMinus8`.
- Validation passed after the token promotion: `@taliya/tokens test`, `@taliya/crm test`, `corepack pnpm typecheck`, and `@taliya/docs build-storybook`.
- Status after product strategy change: `Semi-aprovada`, not approved 1:1. The focused 1:1 blockers above remain useful history, but they are no longer active blockers for this goal unless product review rejects the semi-approved composition or a shared component regression appears.
